text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Carcinogen.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Risk of sensititation</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Not detected by odour unless the conc reaches 10 to 20 times the exposure standard.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">By skin absorption liquid is extremely harmful. Dermatitis occurs.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Exposure to low concentration can cause severe respiratory problems. </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Vapour inhalation of low concentration can cause ASTHMA-like symptoms, sudden acute broncho spasm and Pulmonary Odema. Headache, Neurosis with depression and unconsciousness.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Reacts with moisture In air even at levels as low as 100 ppm, rapidly evolving unstable carbonic acid gases at sufficient rate to rupture cargo tank bulkheads. Insoluble polymeric Urea is formed.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Prolonged heating above 45 C may cause polymerisation. </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Full protective clothing and self contained breathing apparatus when handling hoses,valves,connections.lank cleaning machines etc.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Fire protection/ Alcohol resistant foram, regular foam, water spary ( not into closes tank ), dry chemical</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Although TDI is a hazardous material, the hazard may be minimized if appropriate precautions are observed Typically, there are four routes of potential exposure: inhalation, skin contact, eye contact and ingestion.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Inhalation of TDI vapors may cause irritation of the mucous membranes of the nose, throat or trachea, breathlessness, chest discomfort, difficult breathing and reduced pulmonary function. It is important to avoid exposure above the TLV to minimize the possibility of respiratory sensitization. </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Tests have shown that the least detectable odor level of TDI is approximately 0.2-0.4ppm. This odor</span> <span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">threshold is significantly higher than the OSHA Permissible Exposure Limit (PEL) of 0.02 ceiling. If an</span> <span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">individual can smell TDI, overexposure has most likely occurred. Airborne overexposure, well above the PEL, may result additionally in eye irritation, headache, chemical</span> <span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">bronchitis, asthma-like findings, or pulmonary edema. TDI has also been reported to cause hypersensitivity</span> <span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">pneumonitis, which is characterized by flu-like symptoms, the onset of which may be delayed.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Control of TDI exposure to the recommended guidelines (0.005 ppm as Time-Weighted Average, 0.020 ppm as Short Term Exposure Limit) is believed to protect against sensitization. However, if an individual has become sensitized to TDI, an asthma-like response may then result from very low exposures to TDI. In the event of skin contact, wash thoroughly with soap and flowing water for at least fifteen minutes (A</span> <span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">recent study has indicated that corn oil or polyglycol-based cleaners may remove MDI more effectively than</span> <span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">soap and water, and this may also apply to TDI.(5) Cleaning soon after contamination was also important.).</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Promptly remove all contaminated clothing (including shoes) while washing. If the skin is burned or irritated, seek medical attention. Decontaminate clothing prior to re-use by soaking the garments in an 8 percent ammonia solution for one hour prior to laundering with hot water and detergent. Destroy all contaminated leather items including shoes, belts, and watchbands.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">The&nbsp; easiest and most convenient way to handle spilt TDI is to react it with polyol to produce a</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">low-quality foam, which then can be sold or used as a manufactured product. </span><i><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">(CAUTION: The TDI/polyol reaction is exothermic, which may cause spontaneous combustion.)</span></i><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"> </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Empty TDI drums can be decontaminated by filling them with water or a</span> <span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">decontamination solution (5-10% sodium carbonate) and allowing them to stand unsealed for at least 48</span> <span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">hours.</span><i><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"> WARNING: Under no circumstances should empty drums be burned or cut open with a gas or electric torch, as toxic</span></i><i> </i><i><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">decomposition products may be liberated.</span></i><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"> </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">The use of suitable respiratory equipment is required whenever there is a potential for exposure to airborne TDI levels in excess of permissible exposure limits (PEL 0.02ppm-ceiling, TLV 0.005ppm - 8hour TWA).</span><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">RESISTANCE; ALWAYS CONSULT CARCO HOSE RESISTANCE LIST.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Following hose material is resistant to TDI</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Butyl rubber</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Polyethylene </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Viton rubber</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Teflon ( Hostaflon )</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Chemicals Needed for Cleaning/Personal Protection</span></b><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Low moisture content Chlorinated Solvent MEC (Methylene Chloride ) MARPOL &nbsp;&nbsp;( &nbsp;Y ) , or Trichloroethylene ( Y) or,&nbsp; Perchloroethylene (&nbsp; Y ) approx 8-10 M3 per tank,&nbsp; charterer will supply. If using Methylene chloride ( Dichloro methane ) you will need 15 cum as its evaporation rate is more. Its BP is 40C and SG is 1.34. Some coatings like Phenoline and Devchem 253 are not resistant to MEC.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Sufficient TOLUENE for TDI line filling, say 200 Ltrs for each hose length x 2&nbsp; (loading and discharging)</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Cyanide kit:</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">12 pearls Amyl nitrite.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">2 ampoules Sodium Nnitrite 10CC 3% solution.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">2 ampoules Sodium Thiosulphate 50CC 25% solution.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Crush Amyl Nitrite capsules 5 times at 15 second intervals and hold under nose of a gassed victim.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">200 Ltrs Aqua Ammonia</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">200 Ltrs IPA 30% (Iso<b> </b>propyl alcohol)\u2014to use as solvent if TDI falls on skin.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Two litres of 1% Tincture of<b> </b>Green Soap</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">In case of spill first neutralize it with 50% Ethyl Alcohol, 40% water and 10% conc Ammonia.&nbsp; &nbsp;If spill is small mix with sand or Sodium Bicarbonate. Pack it in a cardboard box and burn it in an open pit using paper as fuel.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">EXTRA EQUIPMENT NEEDED:</span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Sufficient extra hoses (not ships normal hoses) and/or SS pipe&nbsp; enable reach manifold area from pumpstack.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Two SS Spool pieces each with one inch drain valve fitted. ,</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Two SS portable valves for the pumpstack.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Prior to Loading</span></b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">:</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">TDI, Clean tank to<b> </b>water white plus standard</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Pressure test heating coils for leaks, then air blow water condensate from coils, followed by nitrogen blowing to ensure moisture free.&nbsp; Blank off both inlets and returns. The cargo is water reactive and hence ensure NO water comes in contact.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Check/test function of PV Valve</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Air blow PV vent line to ensure no water trapped in Line (especially if slight list or trim).</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Mop dry cargo<b> </b>pump deepwell.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Pressure test cargo pump cofferdam. Purge out cofferdam with nitrogen and fill completely with DOP &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;( Dioctyl Phthalate which has a VD of 13.5).&nbsp; </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Fit pressure gauge to vent line so tank pressure can be monitored during loading, voyage and discharge.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Prepare/connect vapour return system.&nbsp; Calculate Pressure Drop.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Prepare 200 ltrs of neutraliser in case of spills:</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">80 ltrs freshwater, 100 ltrs IPA Iso propyl alcohol , 20 ltrs Aqua Ammonia.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Prepare a solution of 99% IPA and 1% Tincture of Green Soap for personal protection.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Loading&nbsp; TDI or MDI</span></b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Cargo tank will be purged with Nitrogen to minus 40 deg C dew point or 0.25% by shore and pressure may be as high as 10 bars, therefore leave tank cleaning hatch and ullage hatch open as well as PV valve to ensure whole system is purged and tank does not have structural damage due to over pressurization.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">When nitrogen purging is complete and shut down, secure the tank and put PV valve in normal operating position.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Ensure safety shower in operation.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Draeger tubes must be ready for use around the cargo area. Tape off and cordon the loading area.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">When shore ready to start.&nbsp; Open valves at shore connection and pumpstack.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">For TDI you cannot do open ullaging or sampling.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify; text-indent: -0.3in;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; On Completion Loading</span></b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Shore will blow line with nitrogen to tank.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Close all valves and disconnect shore hose and vapour return.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Samples must be taken with closed sampling device.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Fill ships hoses with Toluene using Graco pump. Leave the Toluene inside for 3 days.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Wash hoses with warm water 50-60 C and steamed out and drained.&nbsp; </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Voyage</span></b><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Heat as per charterers instructions by Adjacent Heated Cargo ONLY, unless ship has thermal oil heating,( TDI Normally 35 C ). Do not allow the temp to go below 21C or &gt;45C</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Do NOT have any cold ballast in the double skin.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Maintain nitrogen blanket at positive pressure, minimum 50<b> </b>mb.<b></b></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Discharging</span></b><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Use vapor return hose . DO NOT DISCHARGE</span></b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"> without vapour return hose. </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Inert with N2 while discharging.</span><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Cargo hoses to be blown with shore nitrogen at end of dischg. Fill Chlorinated solvent via manifold from storage cargo tank.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Pre-Cleaning</span></b><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Chlorinated solvent 8-10 M3 of moisture spec &lt;400ppm should already have been loaded into clean extra-dry tank and heated to 30-35 C for TDI ). The chlorinated solvent has to be heated to &gt;MP of the Isocyanate, but <bp itself.=\"\" of=\"\"></bp></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Prepare 2 SS tank cleaning machines and TDI resistant cleaning hoses.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Release ullage hatch but do not lift open, open PV valve. (in case of rapid pressure increase when solvent added.)</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Transfer this solvent to cargo tank via manifold and through cargo hoses with pumpstack valve closed initially to ensure line is totally filled, then opened fully until all solvent transferred into tank.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Disconnect cargo hose from pump stack and connect blind flange with Y for tank&nbsp; cleaning hose to fit. </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Place machines in tank and cover opening to stop any liquid splashing out.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Commence circulation full strength for minimum two hours. Shore to supply Nitrogen continuously during circulation. At this time reconnect shore line (or shore slop line) to ships line ready for use.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">After circulation, disconnect blind with Y and reconnect ships hose to pumpstack, and pump out to shore the Solvent TDI slop. After stripping blow line again with nitrogen, Stop shore nitrogen to tank and batten down tank until at sea.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">When shore hose finally disconnected, fill ships hose/line again with chlorinated solvent as previously done.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">NOTE: IF SHORE IS UNABLE TO ACCEPT THESE CATEGORY&nbsp; Y&nbsp; SLOPS AND THESE ARE BEING TAKEN TO ANOTHER PORT FOR DISPOSAL, REMOVE TANK CLEANING MACHINES AND BATTEN DOWN TANK TO AVOID MOISTURE ENTERING.&nbsp; </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">SLOP SHOULD NOT BE CARRIED FOR LONG PERIODS AS POLYMERISATION CAN OCCUR.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Cleaning at Sea</span></b><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">After the solvent wash\u2014wash the tank with water and detergent as if the solvent was the last cargo. .Make the entries in the Cargo record book. </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Blow out cargo hoses, rig tank cleaning machines.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Blow out DOP from pump cofferdam (overboard) and flush with<b> </b>MEC then blow dry with nitrogen.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">If some Methylene chloride is left in the sump put some Methanol into the tank and keep heating coils crack open.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">First give a cycle cold sea water wash, but above the MP of TDI which is 19.5 deg C.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Then Hot wash tank for 2 hours with sea water.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Give FW rinse .</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Steam tank for 2 hours, then mechanically ventilate for 3 hours.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Test tank with Draeger tube before entering to inspect.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">TDI is a bad previous cargo for PTT and UV test.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">There may be some tough brownish film residue or URETHANE layer ( moisture effect ) which is difficult to remove. Scour with 3m Scotch brite abrasive pads.&nbsp; You may find polymerised bubbles with liquid cargo underneath and will need to neutralise.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">TDI and MDI are extremely poisonous so take no chances, wear the correct safety equipment and do not try to rush the operation of this cargo at any stage.</span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">If Gasoil is used for cleaning ( for TDO only ) , make sure the moisture is &lt;400 ppm at 10 Cum per tank.. Recirc Gasoil for 2 hrs. Toluene can be used for line cleaning.&nbsp; 4 parts of Gasoil are required to dissolve 1 part of TDI.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Loading Arrangement</span></b><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">MANY LENGTHS OF CARGO HOSES WITH PORTABLE VALVE TO BE RIGGED FROM PUMPSTACK HOLE TO SHORE MANIFOLD .&nbsp; DO NOT LOAD THROUGH FIXED SHIPS CARGO LINES . OTHERWISE POLYMERISATION / PLASTIC IN LINES <u>WILL</u> OCCUR.</span></div><div class=\"MsoHeader\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; tab-stops: .5in; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"></span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">&nbsp;</span> </div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Additional equipment required:</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">2 x portable valves</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">1 x blind pumpstack valve</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">2 x SS spool piece with drain valve 1 inch for blowing line and filling hoses with chlorinated solvent after load.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">SUFFICIENT NUMBERS HOSES TO REACH CLOSE TO MANIFOLD AREA.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">########################################</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif; font-size: 14pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">MDI (DIPHENYLMETHANE DIISOCYANATE)</span></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Characteristics&nbsp; MDI</span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Used for making rigid foam.</span><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">CHRIS/ DPM</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Dark coloured liquid with faint tarry odour.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">MP (pure)/ 37.2 deg C</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Specific gravity (liquid)/ 1.197 @ 70 deg C,</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">BP/ 196C</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Coefficient of expansion/0.00098 per degree C</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Vapor density (air= 1.0)/8.5</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Vapor pressure @ 46 C/very low---0.00009 mm HG @25C</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">IMO pollution category/ Y</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">USCG Compatability/Group 12</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">UN number/2489</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">AH/ 60C</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">DH/ 45</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">VH/ 39C</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">TLV/ 0.05 ppm</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">FP/ 218C</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">MDI is not water soluble. Sinks in water</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Viscosity 12 mPas at 40C</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">FOSFA banned</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Incompatible with strong oxidizing agents.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Reacts violently with acids, alcohols and strong acids.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">If inhibited by Ammonia do not stow in zinc tank ( pH &gt;9 ).</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Solubility, - soluble in Acetone and Kerosene</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Flammable at high temperatures. Fire will cause polymerization and dangerously high pressures.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Reacts slowly with water producing C02,(Carbon dioxide),</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Vapor is strong irritant to eyes and throat causing eye and lung injury, even low concentrations cannot be tolerated. On heating MDI gives toxic vapors of Carbon Monoxide, oxides of Nitrogen and Hydro Cyanide gas with very high VP.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">REACTIVITY: MDI is unstable in traces of moisture, slowly forming C02 gas (carbon dioxide)</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">SAFETY: Full protective clothing and self contained breathing apparatus when handling hoses,valves,connections,tank cleaning machines.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Heat as per charterers instructions by Adjacent Heated Cargo ONLY, unless ship has thermal oil heating,</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Fill ships hoses with chlorinated solvent like Perchloroethylene or Methylene chloride for MDI,</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">say 200 Ltrs for each hose length x 2&nbsp; (loading and discharging)</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">At normal unloading and storage temperatures, MDI has a relatively low vapor pressure. With adequate ventilation, airborne MDI vapor concentrations are unlikely to reach or exceed exposure guidelines.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Nevertheless, at elevated temperature, or if MDI is aerosolized by compressed airblow , health problems will result.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Inhalation of MDI may cause irritation of the mucous membranes of the nose, throat or trachea,</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">breathlessness, chest discomfort, difficult breathing and reduced pulmonary function. It is important to avoid exposure above the TLV to minimize the possibility of respiratory sensitization.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Overexposure well above the PEL may result in eye irritation, headache, chemical bronchitis, asthma-like symptoms or pulmonary edema. Diisocyanates have also been reported to cause hypersensitivity</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">pneumonitis, which is characterized by flu-like symptoms, the onset of which may be delayed. Skin contact may result in an irritant or allergic contact dermatitis and may play a role in respiratory sensitization.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Skin staining or discoloration may occur. Long term contact may cause redness, swelling and blistering. Control of MDI exposure to the recommended guidelines (0.005 ppm as Time Weighted Average, 0.020 ppm as Ceiling) is believed to protect against sensitization. However, if an individual has become sensitized to MDI, an asthma-like response may then result from very low exposures</span>. </div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">The ACGIH TLV for MDI is 0.005 ppm</span> <span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">(0.05 mg/m3) as an 8-hour Time Weighted Average (TWA). OSHA requires that exposures be controlled to</span> <span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">below a PEL of 0.02 ppm (0.2 mg/m3) as a ceiling, to prevent lung tumours.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">In the event of skin contact, wash thoroughly with soap and flowing water (</span> <span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">corn oil or polyglycol-based cleaners may remove MDI more effectively than soap and water. Decontaminate clothing prior to re-use by</span> <span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">soaking the garments in an 8 percent ammonia solution for one hour prior to laundering with hot water and</span> <span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">detergent.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">When transferring MDI, personal protective equipment should be worn by</span> <span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">crew engaged in cargo work, tankcleaning</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">This may, depending upon conditions, consist of:</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">\u2022 Chemical goggles;</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">\u2022 Face shield;</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">\u2022 Chemical gloves, resistant to MDI</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">\u2022 Long-sleeve coveralls or full body suit, resistant to MDI</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">\u2022 Fitted boots made of material&nbsp; resistant to MDI, and;</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">\u2022 Head protection, such as a close fitting hood, made of a material resistant to MDI.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">PAPI ( POLYETHYLENE POLYPHENYL ISOCYANATE )</span></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">UN number/ 2206(i) 2207</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">MARPOL category / Y</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">Maintain temperature between 24C and 40C. Do not allow the temperature to go below 18C r&gt; 32C</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 8.5pt;\">CAS / 9016-87-9 0.1-0.5&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 8.5pt;\">OSHA-PEL /&nbsp; TWA- Ceil- 0.020&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-layout-grid-align: none;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 8.5pt;\">ACGIH-TLV /&nbsp; TWA- 0.005 ppm STEL</span><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\"></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQdFtoJ5CDI/AAAAAAAAB7s/SpY_leaREXc/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQdFtoJ5CDI/AAAAAAAAB7s/SpY_leaREXc/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" /></a></div><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL ( 28 years in command )-- POSTED IN PUBLIC INTEREST.</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-pagination: none; text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"font-family: Calibri, sans-serif;\">..</span></div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt.
